         // CHECK FOR SESSION AND HIDE SMART BANNER //
         var smart_session = '';
         //alert(smart_session);
         if ( smart_session == 'true' ) {
            //$('#smart_banner').remove();
         }
         else {
         
         
         // CHECK UA AND ADJUST CONDINGLY //
            var ua = navigator.userAgent;
            var checker = {
                    android: ua.match(/Android/),
                    apple: ua.match(/iPhone/),
                    windows: ua.match(/Windows/)
            };    
               if ( checker.apple ) {
                 $(".smart_banner_link").attr('href','https://itunes.apple.com/gb/app/funkypigeon.com/id441509555?mt=8');
                 }

               if ( checker.android ) {
                 $(".smart_banner_link").attr('href','https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.red7mobile.funky.pigeon.v2&hl=en_GB');
                 }
               
               if ( checker.windows ) {
                 $(".smart_banner_link").attr('href','https://www.windowsphone.com/en-gb/store/app/funky-pigeon/0285c62f-4abb-46c8-8285-964665d13ccb');
                 }
            }
 
            $( "#smart_close" ).click(function() {
                 $(".smart_banner" ).slideToggle( "slow", function() {});
                 $("#mobile").animate({ 'marginTop': '0'}, "slow");
                 $.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    url: "/Pages/MobileSessionUpdate.aspx",
                    data: "{}",
                    dataType: "html",
                    success: function(result){}
                });   
            });
                
            $( document ).ready(function() {
                var smart_session = '';
                 if ( smart_session != 'true' ) {
                    $("#mobile").addClass("mobileSmartBannerMargin");
                 }else{
                    $("#mobile").removeClass("mobileSmartBannerMargin");
                 }
            });
        </script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript"> 
    /*document.onclick=WindowClickEventExplorer;*/ 
    function TopMenuClick(value, objname) {
        var pageName = "";
       
        switch (value) {
            case 'card':
                {
                    pageName = "PersonalisedCards.aspx";
                    break;
                }
            case 'calendar':
                {
                    //pageName = "PersonalisedCalendars.aspx";
                    pageName = "PhotoCalendar.aspx?branding=photocalendar&color=grey&type=calendar";
                    break;
                }
            case 'poster':
                {
                    pageName = "PersonalisedPosters.aspx";
                    break;
                }
                
            case 'WallArt':
                {
                    pageName = "WallArt.aspx";
                    break;
                }
                
            case 'gift':
                {
                    pageName = "Gifts.aspx";
                    break;
                }
            case 'notebook':
                {
                    pageName = "PersonalisedNotebooks.aspx";
                    break;
                }
            case 'flower':
                {
                    pageName = "PersonalisedFlowers.aspx";
                    break;
                }
            case 'photobooks':
                {
                    pageName = "Pages/Photobooks/PhotoBooks.aspx";
                    break;
                }
            case 'cases':
                {
                    pageName = "PhoneCases.aspx";
                    break;
                }
            case 't-shirts':
                {
                    pageName = "PersonalisedTshirts.aspx";
                    break;
                }
            case 'bouquets':
                {
                    pageName = "PersonalisedFlowers.aspx";
                    break;
                }
            case 'postcards':
                {
                    pageName = "Pages/Branding/PhotoPostcards.aspx?branding=photopostcards&color=grey&type=postcards";
                    break;
                }    
                
            case 'iframeSG':
                {
                    pageName = "Gifts.aspx";
                    break;
                }
            case 'join':
                {
                    pageName = "Pages/MyAccount.aspx";
                    break;
                }
            case 'login':
                {
                    pageName = "Pages/CustomerLogin.aspx";
                    break;
                }
            case 'logout':
                {
                    pageName = "Pages/CustomerLogin.aspx?logoff=true";
                    break;
                }

            case 'register':
                {
                    pageName = "Pages/CustomerAdd.aspx";
                    break;
                }

            default:
                {
                    pageName = "Personalised.aspx";
                    break;
                }
        }
       
        if (pageName.length > 0) {
            //alert(value);
            if (value == "calendar")
            window.document.location = "http://www.funkypigeon.com/" + pageName;
        else if (pageName.indexOf("?logoff=true", 0) > 0)
            window.document.location = "http://www.funkypigeon.com/" + pageName + "&type=" + value;
        else
            window.document.location = "http://www.funkypigeon.com/" + pageName + "?type=" + value;
        } else {
            NormalizeAllMenu();
            document.getElementById(objname).className = 'topMenuItemSelected';
            CallServer(value, "");
        }

    }

    //function displayResult(rValue) {
        //if (document.getElementById('ctl00_uclHeader1_divCardLinkTop') != null) {
            //document.getElementById('ctl00_uclHeader1_divCardLinkTop').innerHTML = rValue;
        //}
   // }

    function NormalizeAllMenu() {
        document.getElementById('tdTopMenuCards').className = 'topMenuItem';
        document.getElementById('tdTopMenuCalendar').className = 'topMenuItem';
        document.getElementById('tdTopMenuPoster').className = 'topMenuItem';
        document.getElementById('tdTopMenuGift').className = 'topMenuItem';
        document.getElementById('tdTopMenuJoin').className = 'topMenuItem';
        document.getElementById('tdTopMenuLogin').className = 'topMenuItem';
    }

    function swapClassTopMenu(sType, classID) {
        /*if(sType==1) {
        document.getElementById('topmenuA' + classID).className = 'lnk_active'; 
        document.getElementById('topmenuL' + classID).className = 'active';}
        else {
        document.getElementById('topmenuA' + classID).className = 'lnk_normal';
        document.getElementById('topmenuL' + classID).className = 'normal';}*/
    }
    /*
    function WindowClickEventExplorer(e){
    document.getElementById('ctl00_uclHeader1_divCardLinkTop').innerHTML =''; }

function CancelAutoClose(evt){
    if (window.event){
    window.event.cancelBubble = true; }
    else {
    evt.cancelBubble = true; }
    }
    */
    function restrictKeyCode() {
        if (event.keyCode == 190 || event.keyCode == 188)
            return false;
        else
            return true;
    }

    function showInvalidImage() {
        alert('Invalid image file format. We currently only support BMP,TIF,JPG,JPEG,GIF,PNG');
    }

    function ValidateFileType(filePath, imgUploadButId) {
        var ext = filePath.substring(filePath.lastIndexOf('.'), filePath.length);
        var flag = false;

        if (ext.toLowerCase() == ".jpg") {
            flag = true;
        }
        else if (ext.toLowerCase() == ".jpeg") {
            flag = true;
        }
        else if (ext.toLowerCase() == ".gif") {
            flag = true;
        }
        else if (ext.toLowerCase() == ".bmp") {
            flag = true;
        }
        else if (ext.toLowerCase() == ".tiff") {
            flag = true;
        }
        else if (ext.toLowerCase() == ".png") {
            flag = true;
        }

        if (flag == false) {
            showInvalidImage();
            document.getElementById(imgUploadButId).disabled = true;
        }
        else {
            document.getElementById(imgUploadButId).disabled = false;
        }
    }

    function showCountryList() {
        document.getElementById('flag_reveal').style.display = "block";
    }
 
</script>

		                        function readMoreText () {
		                            var reveal_start_height = $('.seotext').height();
		                            var reveal_height = $('.seotext').attr('id');
		                            
		                            $('.hide').hide();
		                            
		                            $('.readmore').click( function(){
			                            $('.seotext').animate({
				                            'height' : reveal_height
			                            });
			                            $(this).hide();
			                            $('.hide').show();
		                            });
		                            
		                            $('.hide').click(function(){
			                            $('.seotext').animate({
				                            'height' : reveal_start_height
				                        });
				                        $('.readmore').show();
				                        $(this).hide();
			                        });
		                        }

				                $('.tab_links').hide();
				                $('#birthday').show();
				                

                    				
		                    });

        getMobileOperatingSystem();
        
        function getMobileOperatingSystem() {
          var userAgent = navigator.userAgent || navigator.vendor || window.opera;

          if( userAgent.match( /iPad/i ) || userAgent.match( /iPhone/i ) || userAgent.match( /iPod/i ) )
          {
            $('.ios_warning').show();
          }
          
          if( userAgent.match( /iPad/i ))
          {
            $('.ios_warning').addClass('warning_ipad');
          }
          
        }

			        $(tab_link_name).show();

            //== OPEN/CLOSE MENU FUNCTIONS
            function openMobileMenu () {
		        $('#mobile').css({'position':'relative'});
                $('#mobile').animate({'right':'275px'}, { "duration": 400 });
                $('#header').animate({'right':'275px'}, { "duration": 400 });
                $('.smart_banner').animate({'right':'275px'}, { "duration": 400 });
                $('.smart_banner').css({'top':'0'});
                $('#mobile_side_menu').animate({'right':'0px'}, { "duration": 400 });
                $('.mobile_menu').hide();
                $('.mobile_menu_close').css({'display':'block'});
                $('#mobile_side_menu').addClass('full_height');
		    }
		    
		    function closeMobileMenu () {
		        $('#mobile').animate({'right':'0px'}, { "duration": 400 });
		        $('#header').animate({'right':'0px'}, { "duration": 400 });
		        $('.smart_banner').animate({'right':'0px'}, { "duration": 400 });
                $('#mobile_side_menu').animate({'right':'-275px'}, { "duration": 400 });
                $('.mobile_menu_close').removeClass('refine_menu_close');
                $('.mobile_menu_close').hide();
                $('.mobile_menu').css({'display':'block'});
		    }
		    
		    function openRefineMenu () {
		        $('.MobileNavHolder').hide();
                $('#left_nav_home').show();
                openMobileMenu();
                
                $('.search_refine_grey').animate({'left':'-274px'}, {"duration":400, queue:false })
                $('.search_refine_grey').fadeIn();
                
                $('.search_refine_btn').hide();
                $('.search_refine_btn_active').show();
                
                $('.mobile_menu_close').addClass('refine_menu_close');
                $('.msm_header .msm_header_title').html('Refine Results...');
                $('.msm_header .msm_header_title').append('<div class="RefineCloseBtn">Close</div>');
                
                $('.RefineCloseBtn').click(function(){
                    closeMobileMenu();
                    closeRefineMenu(); 
                });
		    }
            
            function closeRefineMenu () {
		        $('.search_refine_grey').animate({'left':'0px'}, {"duration":400, queue:false })
                $('.search_refine_grey').fadeOut();
                
                $('.search_refine_btn_active').hide();
                $('.search_refine_btn').show();
		        
		        setTimeout(function() {
                    $('.MobileNavHolder').show();
                    $('.msm_header .msm_header_title').html("I'm Looking For...");
                    $('.RefineCloseBtn').remove();
                }, 500);
		    }

                $('.notification').css('opacity','0');

	        $(window).scroll(function() {
                var ScrollHeightNav = $('#left-col').height();
		        
		        //== ADD CLASS FIXED NAV
		        if ($(window).scrollTop() > 206) {
			        $('.nav').addClass('visible');
		        }
		        else {
		           $('.nav').removeClass('visible');
		        } 
		        //== ADD CLASS SCROLL (TABLET LEFT NAV)
		        if ($(window).scrollTop() > 245) {
			        $('.mobileLeftNavBtn').addClass('scroll');
		        }
		        else {
		           $('.mobileLeftNavBtn').removeClass('scroll');
		        } 
		        //== ADD CLASS CLOSEFIXED (TABLET LEFT NAV)
		        if ($(window).scrollTop() > ScrollHeightNav + 245 ) {
			        $('.mobileLeftNavBtn').addClass('closeFixed');
		        }
		        else {
		           $('.mobileLeftNavBtn').removeClass('closeFixed');
		        } 
		          			
	        });
    		
    		
	        //== SEARCH WHEN YOU PRESS ENTER
	        
	        //SEARCH BAR TEXT REMOVE
	        
	        function searchFieldValidation() {
                var searchValue = $('#ctl00_uclHeader1_tbSearch').val();
		        if ( searchValue == "I'm searching for..." || ($.trim( searchValue )).length==0 ) {
		            $('.search_tip_reveal').fadeIn();
		            //alert('type a search term');
		        }
		        else {$('#ctl00_uclHeader1_imageButtontomMenuSearch').trigger('click');}
		        //alert(searchValue);
            
            }
    		
	        //== FIXED NAV
	        $('input.fixed_nav_search').keypress(function(event){
              if(event.keyCode == 13){
                $('#ctl00_uclHeader1_imageButtontomFixedMenuSearch').trigger('click');
              }
            });
            
            //== MOBILE SEARCH
	        $('input.topMenuSearchText').keypress(function(event){
              if(event.keyCode == 13){
                $('#ctl00_uclHeader1_imageButtontomMobileSearch').click();
                event.preventDefault();
              }
            });
            
            // detect touch
           if(('ontouchstart' in window) || (navigator.msMaxTouchPoints > 0)){
                  document.documentElement.className += " touch";
           }
           
           closeDDMenu();
           
           function closeDDMenu() {
                $('.close_touch_menu').click(function(){
                    $('.dd').hide();
                    //$('.staticNav li').removeClass('nav_hover_active');
                    //$('html').trigger( "click" );
                    //$('#header')[0].click();
                    $('.dd').addClass('touchNavActive');
                    //alert('Touched');
                });
           }
           
           openTabletMenu();
           
           function openTabletMenu() {
                $('#top_nav li').hover(function(){
                    $('.dd').removeClass('touchNavActive');
                });
           }
           
           // MOBILE BREADCRUMB BACK BUTTON
           function mobileGoBack() {
                window.history.back()
           }
           
           // CHECK IF FACEBOOK LOGIN EXISTS
           function FBSignOnExists() {
                if ($('.facebook_bday_list').length > 0){
                    $('#template_wrapper').addClass('fb_login');
                    //alert('Facebook Login Exists');
                }
           }

           FBSignOnExists();
           
           // HINTS AND TIPS SCRIPT
           $('body').HintsAndTips();
       //}
       
        
        
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    //var ua = navigator.userAgent, 
    //event = (ua.match(/iPhone/i)) ? "touchend" : "click";
	
	//MOBILE MENU - LINK CLICK
	$('.FirstMenu a').click(function(){
		$('.FirstMenu').animate({'left':'-100%'}, {duration:200, queue:false });
		$('.SecondMenu').animate({'right':'0%'}, {duration:200, queue:false,
		    complete: function() {
		      $('.FirstMenu').hide();
		    }
		});
		
		var clickedId = $(this).attr('id');
		$('#' + clickedId + 'SM').addClass('active');
		
		var subNavHeight = $('.subNav.active').height();
		$('.MobileNav').height(subNavHeight + 60);
		
	});
	
	//MOBILE MENU - BACK BTN
	$('a.Backbtn').click(function(){
		$('.MobileNav').height('720px');
		$('.FirstMenu').show();
		$('.FirstMenu').animate({'left':'0%'}, {duration:200, queue:false });
		$('.SecondMenu').animate({'right':'-100%'}, {duration:200, queue:false,
		    complete: function() {
		      $('.subNav').removeClass('active');
		    }
		});
	});
	
</script>

</div>
